<div id="review_57929008" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/57929008" />
    <a title="Marleen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1616365-marleen"><img alt="Marleen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576835511p2/1616365.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/57929008?book_show_action=true">Oct 23, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marleen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marleen" href="/user/show/1616365-marleen">Marleen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18873900-hide">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1616365-marleen?shelf=lisa-gardner">lisa-gardner</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer57929008" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4787363502519806493">Hide is one of my favorite Lisa Gardner books, because it doesn’t present us with chapters where, we, as readers, are confronted with the evil thoughts of the murderer. I prefer a book focusing on the investigation, the investigators and the possible victims and their families. I love police procedural, and this was a good one. I am so tired of books where we are in the mind of those perpetrators. There’s too many of them. It’s tedious - and what's the upside, I ask you? Unfortunately, Lisa Gard</span>
  <span id="freeText4787363502519806493" style="display:none">Hide is one of my favorite Lisa Gardner books, because it doesn’t present us with chapters where, we, as readers, are confronted with the evil thoughts of the murderer. I prefer a book focusing on the investigation, the investigators and the possible victims and their families. I love police procedural, and this was a good one. I am so tired of books where we are in the mind of those perpetrators. There’s too many of them. It’s tedious - and what's the upside, I ask you? Unfortunately, Lisa Gardner does that same thing in her following books. So yes those are not as good in my opinion.<br />This book is all about unraveling a mystery - and I absolutely enjoyed the enigma that involves Annabelle’s family. For the longest time from the age of seven, her life has been about running. Her parents moved around so much, escaping some unknown danger, leaving one city for another, at the drop of a hat. Now Annabelle, at the age of thirty-two, under the name Tanya, lives in Boston again, her parents deceased. When police discover an underground chamber on the grounds of a derelict mental institute, containing six bodies, one of the young victims has a necklace with Annabelle’s full name on her. <br />The good thing about this story is that we really don’t know who the bad guy is until the very end. What I also enjoyed is that we see Bobby Dodge return, this time as a State Police detective. <br />Bobby joins the investigation at D.D. Warren's request. Bobby’s friendship with D.D. Warren is a longstanding one and their banter is very entertaining. Finally, I am glad that Bobby and Annabelle became interested in each other. Their coming together was a bit more subtle and promising.<br />Over the next books, we get little snippets about how Annabelle and Bobby are doing. I hope Lisa Gardner will consider a story where Bobby Dodge takes on a more prominent role again.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4787363502519806493" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

<span id="freeTextContainer12322935347622442421">Unbelievable.<br/><br/>Never believe anything Lisa Gardner tells you. You may think she is being straight with you but, take my word for it, she is not to be trusted. She will change her story. <i>Hide</i> is the second book of hers that I have read and the second time she has mislead me repeatedly. If I didn’t know better, I’d say she is an unrepentant suspense mystery writer!<br/><br/>She is so unbelievable, that she gets five stars from me for <i>Hide</i> and I am immediately going to start reading the third book in the serie</span>
  <span id="freeText12322935347622442421" style="display:none">Unbelievable.<br /><br />Never believe anything Lisa Gardner tells you. You may think she is being straight with you but, take my word for it, she is not to be trusted. She will change her story. <i>Hide</i> is the second book of hers that I have read and the second time she has mislead me repeatedly. If I didn’t know better, I’d say she is an unrepentant suspense mystery writer!<br /><br />She is so unbelievable, that she gets five stars from me for <i>Hide</i> and I am immediately going to start reading the third book in the series, <i>The Neighbor</i>. <br /></span>

She kinda kicks ass!</span>

<div id="review_1893698881" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1893698881" />
    <a title="Teresa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15654040-teresa"><img alt="Teresa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1510501152p2/15654040.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1893698881?book_show_action=true">Jul 15, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Teresa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Teresa" href="/user/show/15654040-teresa">Teresa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1893698881" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7984852496444972724">This was one of those books that hooked me from page one. The first chapter introduced such an interesting character and premise, I couldn't flip the pages fast enough to find out more. And as the book went on, it became more complicated, twisty, and one giant puzzle. Just when I thought I had some ideas, something else would throw a wrench in my theory. This is everything I love about reading mystery and suspense.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('oa9w5ob8xINmsKnsCRdX4d/sBWzTypyoRhVWD33sHfpC1AfZ0gOEgcwmF+NQNZ7zWgNQioUsSfxe1n2fx64FWA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ZWXDWLrKsGtb6hG/dWmX0nbHfXhSXPRMwo4fwoSlzHyGHrRn7jXwafF8r7AsS17A8ygongS6IRjaTTRSPufU3g==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer17211599814764449968">Lisa Gardner is a #1 <i>New York Times</i> bestselling crime novelist. A self-described research junkie, she has parlayed her interest in police procedure and twisted minds into a streak of twenty-plus thrillers. Her latest, BEFORE SHE DISAPPEARED, is available January 19, 2021.<br/><br/>Meet Frankie Elkin, an everyday, average person who specializes in finding missing people. When the locals have given up, when t</span>
  <span id="freeText17211599814764449968" style="display:none">Lisa Gardner is a #1 <i>New York Times</i> bestselling crime novelist. A self-described research junkie, she has parlayed her interest in police procedure and twisted minds into a streak of twenty-plus thrillers. Her latest, BEFORE SHE DISAPPEARED, is available January 19, 2021.<br /><br />Meet Frankie Elkin, an everyday, average person who specializes in finding missing people. When the locals have given up, when the media has never bothered to care, Frankie takes on the challenge. Her latest mission has brought her to Mattapan, Boston, to find a missing Haitian teen. Eleven months later, Angelique Badeau's disappearance remains a mystery. What happened to the quiet, studious teen? Frankie learns quickly the dangers of asking too many questions, but that won't stop her from learning the truth behind what happened <i>before she disappeared</i>.<br /><br />Lisa lives in the mountains of New Hampshire with two crazy pups and an ancient rescue dog. When not writing, Lisa loves to hike, play cribbage, and, of course, read!<br /></span>
